# Platform-Wide Terminology Tracking

**Created**: 2025-11-27
**Updated**: 2025-12-03 (Added Treasure Hunt Finnish analysis - 7 violations fixed, Subtraction Finnish - 12 violations fixed, Prepositions Finnish - 2 violations fixed, Draw-and-Color Finnish - 10 violations fixed, Big-small Finnish - 12 violations fixed, Writing Norwegian - 3 violations fixed, Writing Finnish - 2 violations fixed)
**Purpose**: Track terminology standards and ensure cross-app consistency
**Apps Analyzed**: 14/33 Spanish, 14/33 Italian, 19/33 Portuguese (Brazilian), 20/33 Dutch, 7/33 Danish, 10/33 Swedish, 32/33 Norwegian, 16/33 Finnish
**Norwegian Apps**: 32 apps analyzed - Writing added 2025-12-02 (all 32 apps use platform standards)
**Spanish Apps**: Sudoku, Big-Small, Chart Count, Draw-and-Color, Find Objects, Grid Match, Math Puzzle, Missing Pieces, Pattern Train, Pattern Worksheet, Picture Pathway, Picture Sort, Prepositions, Shadow Match, Treasure Hunt, Word Guess
**Italian Apps**: Wordsearch, Find and Count, Crossword, Drawing Lines, Math Puzzle, Picture Pathway, Odd One Out, Pattern Train, Treasure Hunt, Writing, (4 more analyzed)
**Portuguese (Brazilian) Apps**: Wordsearch, Addition, Alphabet Train, Coloring, Drawing Lines, Math Worksheet, Word Scramble, Find and Count, Matchup Maker, Picture Bingo, Big-Small, Find Objects, Grid Match, Crossword, Missing Pieces, Odd One Out, Pattern Train, Picture Sort, Shadow Match, Writing
**Dutch Apps**: Wordsearch, Math Worksheet, Find and Count, Matchup Maker, Drawing Lines, Picture Bingo, Sudoku, Big-Small, Chart Count, Draw and Color, Find Objects, Grid Match, Cryptogram, More-Less, Odd One Out, Pattern Train, Pattern Worksheet, Picture Sort, Subtraction, Treasure Hunt
**Danish Apps**: Find and Count, Matchup Maker, Chart Count, Math Puzzle, More-Less, Pattern Worksheet, Prepositions (+ 14 apps fixed retroactively: Addition, Alphabet Train, Math Worksheet, Wordsearch, Word Scramble, Grid Match, Word Guess, Sudoku, Missing Pieces, Cryptogram, Crossword, Treasure Hunt)
**Swedish Apps**: Find and Count, Matchup Maker, Sudoku, Big-Small, Chart Count, Draw and Color, Crossword, Pattern Train, Picture Pathway, Word Guess
**Finnish Apps**: Wordsearch, Addition, Alphabet Train, Coloring, Find and Count, Drawing Lines, Picture Bingo, Big-Small, Draw and Color, Pattern Train, Picture-Pathway, Picture-Sort, Prepositions, Subtraction, Treasure Hunt, Writing (16 apps - all platform compliant)

## üá≥üá± DUTCH / NEDERLANDS STANDARDS

### Dutch - "Generate"

**PLATFORM STANDARD**: **"Maken"** (Changed 2025-11-29)
**PREVIOUS STANDARD**: "Genereren" (Apps 1-4, before retroactive change)

**RATIONALE FOR CHANGE**:
- **More user-friendly** than technical "Genereren"
- Better aligns with platform philosophy: "User-friendly over technical"
- More natural Dutch for target audience (kindergarten teachers)
- Multiple RATIONALEs independently recommended "Maken" (Addition, Drawing Lines, Find and Count)
- Consistent with Spanish using "Crear" (natural over technical)
- SOURCE: Addition RATIONALE (Maken is "more natural and direct"), Drawing Lines RATIONALE (Maken is "simple, clear action")

**APPS ANALYZED** (20/33):
- ‚úÖ Wordsearch RATIONALE: Originally recommended "Genereren"
- ‚úÖ Wordsearch ACTUAL: Uses "Maken" ‚úì **RETROACTIVELY UPDATED** (line 1362, changed from "Genereren" ‚Üí "Maken", 2025-11-29)
- ‚úÖ Math Worksheet RATIONALE: Uses "Werkbladgenerator" in title
- ‚úÖ Math Worksheet ACTUAL: Uses "Maken" ‚úì **RETROACTIVELY UPDATED** (lines 1387-1389, changed from "Genereren" ‚Üí "Maken", 2025-11-29)
- ‚úÖ Find and Count RATIONALE: Recommends "Maken" (line 59: "Simple, clear Dutch")
- ‚úÖ Find and Count ACTUAL: Uses "Maken" ‚úì **RETROACTIVELY UPDATED** (lines 959-961, changed from "Genereren" ‚Üí "Maken", 2025-11-29)
- ‚úÖ Matchup Maker RATIONALE: Originally recommended "Genereren"
- ‚úÖ Matchup Maker ACTUAL: Uses "Maken" ‚úì **RETROACTIVELY UPDATED** (line 1340, changed from "Genereren" ‚Üí "Maken", 2025-11-29)
- ‚úÖ Addition RATIONALE: Recommends "Maken" (explicit: "Natuurlijker en directer dan 'genereren' voor knoppen")
- ‚úÖ Drawing Lines RATIONALE: Recommends "Maken" (line 55: "Simple, clear action")
- ‚úÖ Drawing Lines ACTUAL: Uses "Maken" ‚úì Correctly implements RATIONALE (line 1289)
- ‚úÖ Picture Bingo ACTUAL: Uses "Maken" ‚úì Correctly aligned (line 1148)
- ‚úÖ Sudoku ACTUAL: Uses "Maken" ‚úì Correctly aligned with platform standard (lines 1497-1499, 1527)
- ‚úÖ Big-Small RATIONALE: Recommends "Genereren/Maken" (both used contextually, line 69)
- ‚úÖ Big-Small ACTUAL: Uses "Maken" ‚úì Correctly aligned with platform standard (lines 1128-1130)
- ‚úÖ Chart Count ACTUAL: Uses "Maken" ‚úì Correctly aligned with platform standard (lines 1230-1232)
- ‚úÖ Draw and Color ACTUAL: Uses "Maken" ‚úì Correctly aligned with platform standard (line 959)
- ‚úÖ Find Objects ACTUAL: Uses "Maken" ‚úì Correctly aligned with platform standard (line 1431)
- ‚úÖ Grid Match ACTUAL: Uses "Maken" ‚úì **FIXED** to platform standard (line 1237, was already correct; line 1273 fixed from "Genereer" ‚Üí "Maak")
- ‚úÖ Cryptogram ACTUAL: Uses "Maken" ‚úì **ALREADY CORRECT** - aligned with platform standard (line 585)
- ‚úÖ Missing Pieces RATIONALE: Recommended "Genereren" (line 72: listed under "Technische Precisie")
- ‚úÖ Missing Pieces ACTUAL: Uses "Maken" ‚úì **ALIGNED** with platform standard (lines 1409-1411, 1419, 1431-1437, 1472, aligned during RATIONALE application 2025-11-29)
- ‚ö†Ô∏è More-Less RATIONALE: **INCORRECTLY** recommended "Genereren" (line 297: conflicts with platform standard!)
- ‚úÖ More-Less ACTUAL: Uses "Maken" ‚úì **ALREADY CORRECT** - aligned with platform standard (lines 2082-2084, 2130, 2134, 2168, 2170, 2183, 2190, 2224-2225, 2276, 2299-2301), **RATIONALE OVERRIDDEN** by platform standard
- ‚úÖ Odd One Out RATIONALE: Recommends "Maken" (line 103: "Natuurlijker dan 'Genereren'")
- ‚úÖ Odd One Out ACTUAL: Uses "Maken" ‚úì **ALREADY CORRECT** - aligned with platform standard (line 1063)
- ‚ö†Ô∏è Pattern Train RATIONALE: Recommends "Genereren" (professional translation line 130: conflicts with platform standard!)
- ‚úÖ Pattern Train ACTUAL: Uses "Maken" ‚úì **FIXED** to platform standard (lines 1163-1165, changed "Genereren" ‚Üí "Maken" in generate.answer and generate.worksheet, 2025-11-29)
- ‚úÖ Pattern Worksheet RATIONALE: Recommends "Maken" (professional translation line 120: "Natuurlijker dan Genereren")
- ‚úÖ Pattern Worksheet ACTUAL: Uses "Maken" ‚úì **ALREADY CORRECT** - aligned with platform standard (lines 1119-1121, verified 2025-11-29)
- ‚ö†Ô∏è Prepositions RATIONALE: Not explicitly discussed (implied "Maken" through "Generate" section)
- ‚úÖ Prepositions ACTUAL: Uses "Maken" ‚úì **ALREADY CORRECT** - aligned with platform standard (line 1049, verified 2025-11-29)
- ‚ö†Ô∏è Subtraction RATIONALE: Recommends "Genereren" (conflicts with platform standard!)
- ‚úÖ Subtraction ACTUAL: Uses "Maken" ‚úì **ALREADY CORRECT** - aligned with platform standard (lines 1215-1216, 1254-1256, 1290, verified 2025-11-30)
- ‚úÖ Treasure Hunt RATIONALE: Recommends "Maken" (line 354: standard in Dutch software, "Genereren" is familiar but "Maken" is natural)
- ‚úÖ Treasure Hunt ACTUAL: Uses "Maken" ‚úì **ALREADY CORRECT** - aligned with platform standard (lines 960, 984-986, verified 2025-11-30)

**STATUS**: ‚úÖ Platform standard **REVISED** to "Maken" - All 20 apps now aligned

**RETROACTIVE STANDARDIZATION APPLIED** (2025-11-29):
1. Wordsearch: Line 1362: "Genereren" ‚Üí "Maken"
2. Math Worksheet: Lines 1387-1389: "Genereren" ‚Üí "Maken" (3 instances)
3. Find and Count: Lines 959-961: "Genereren" ‚Üí "Maken" (3 instances)
4. Matchup Maker: Line 1340: "Genereren" ‚Üí "Maken"

**IMPLEMENTATION NOTES**:
- Use "Maken" for button labels (e.g., button text)
- Use "gemaakt" or "aangemaakt" in success messages (e.g., "Werkblad succesvol gemaakt!")
- Use "maken" in loading messages (e.g., "Werkblad maken...")
- Use "maken" in informal error messages (e.g., "Maak eerst een werkblad")
- Consistent natural Dutch throughout (button, messages, errors all use "maken" family)

**COMPARISON WITH OTHER LANGUAGES**:
- Spanish: Uses "Crear" (create - natural language choice)
- Dutch: Uses "Maken" (make/create - natural language choice)
- ‚úÖ **CONSISTENT PATTERN**: Both prioritize natural, user-friendly over technical

**PLATFORM PHILOSOPHY ALIGNMENT**: ‚úÖ EXCELLENT
- Prioritizes user-friendly over technical ‚úì
- More appropriate for kindergarten teachers ‚úì
- More natural Dutch ‚úì
- Consistent across language families ‚úì

### Dutch - "Opacity"

**PLATFORM STANDARD**: **"Transparantie"**

**RATIONALE**:
- More user-friendly than technical "dekking" or "opaciteit"
- Better for non-technical kindergarten teachers
- Standard term in Dutch educational software
- SOURCE: Wordsearch RATIONALE line 60 (explicit: "Gebruiksvriendelijker dan 'dekking' of 'opaciteit'")

**APPS ANALYZED** (20/33):
- ‚úÖ Wordsearch RATIONALE: Recommends "Transparantie"

### Dutch - "Grid"

**PLATFORM STANDARD**: **"Rooster"** (for word-based grids)
**APP-SPECIFIC VARIATION**: **"Raster"** (for visual pattern grids)

**RATIONALE**:
- "Rooster" is the standard Dutch term for structured grids (word grids, schedules)
- "Raster" is more appropriate for visual/geometric pattern grids
- CONTEXT-DEPENDENT choice based on app purpose
- SOURCE: Wordsearch RATIONALE line 69 (explicit: "Rooster" is de standaardterm for word grids)

**APPS ANALYZED** (10/33):
- ‚úÖ Wordsearch RATIONALE: Recommends "Rooster" (word grid context)
- ‚úÖ Wordsearch ACTUAL: Uses "Rooster" ‚úì Correctly implements RATIONALE (lines 1298, 1402, fixed from "Raster"/"raster")
- ‚ö†Ô∏è Find and Count RATIONALE: Not explicitly discussed
- ‚úÖ Find and Count ACTUAL: Uses "Rooster" ‚úì Correctly implements platform standard (lines 995, 1019, FIXED from "Raster")
- ‚úÖ Grid Match RATIONALE: Recommends "Raster" (visual grid pattern context)
- ‚úÖ Grid Match ACTUAL: Uses "Raster" ‚úì **CORRECT** app-specific choice (lines 1150, 1153, 1263, 1286-1289, 1312) - justified for visual pattern matching

**STATUS**: ‚úÖ Context-dependent standard established
- "Rooster" for word/text grids ‚úì
- "Raster" for visual/pattern grids ‚úì

**RETROACTIVE FIXES APPLIED**:
- 2025-11-29: Wordsearch line 1298: Changed "Rastergrootte" ‚Üí "Roostergrootte"
- 2025-11-29: Wordsearch line 1402: Changed "raster" ‚Üí "rooster" (consistency)
- 2025-11-29: Find and Count line 995: Changed "Rasterafmetingen" ‚Üí "Roosterafmetingen"
- 2025-11-29: Find and Count line 1019: Changed "Het raster" ‚Üí "Het rooster" (consistency)

### Dutch - "Image Library"

**PLATFORM STANDARD**: **"Afbeeldingenverzameling"** (REVISED 2025-11-29)

**PREVIOUS STANDARD**: "Afbeeldingenbibliotheek" (Apps 1-2)

**RATIONALE FOR CHANGE**:
- "Verzameling" is warmer and more accessible for kindergarten teachers
- Better alignment with platform philosophy (user-friendly over formal/technical)
- "Bibliotheek" is more formal/professional but less warm for educational context
- Discovered superior alternative in Find and Count RATIONALE line 84

| Outline | Omtrek | - | Wordsearch RATIONALE line 59 |
| Worksheet | Werkblad | Oefenblad | Wordsearch RATIONALE line 29 |

| Clear All | Alles wissen | Alles verwijderen | Wordsearch RATIONALE line 32 |
| Allow Reverse | Achterwaartse | Omgekeerde | Wordsearch RATIONALE line 71 |
| Puzzle (math) | Opgave | Puzzel | Math Worksheet RATIONALE line 84 |
| Grayscale | Grijstinten | Grijswaarden, Grijsschaal | Math Worksheet RATIONALE line 74 |

**Formality**: Always informal "je/jouw" (never formal "u/uw")
**Placeholders**: Always "bijv:" (colon, no space)

## Spanish - "Worksheet"

**PLATFORM STANDARD**: **"Hoja de ejercicios"**

**RATIONALE**:
- Standard term in Spanish schools and educational software
- Not "p√°gina" or "ficha"
- SOURCE: Sudoku quality notes

**APPS ANALYZED** (8/33):
- ‚úÖ Sudoku ACTUAL: Uses "Hoja de ejercicios" ‚úì
- ‚úÖ Addition ACTUAL: Uses "Ficha" (inconsistent with Sudoku)
- ‚úÖ Big-Small ACTUAL: Uses "Ficha de trabajo" (inconsistent with both)
- ‚úÖ Chart Count ACTUAL: Updated to "Ficha" (was "Hoja de trabajo") (lines 588, 676, 679, 681, 687, 699)
- ‚úÖ Draw-and-Color ACTUAL: Updated to "Ficha" (was "Hoja de ejercicios") (line 547)
- ‚úÖ Grid Match ACTUAL: Updated to "Ficha" (was "Hoja de trabajo") (lines 623, 676, 678, 681, 683, 688, 690, 704, 706, 747, 759, 760)
- ‚úÖ Missing Pieces ACTUAL: Updated to "Ficha" (was "Ficha de trabajo") (lines 735-736, 761-762, 800, 814, 839)
- ‚úÖ Pattern Train ACTUAL: Uses "Ficha de trabajo" ‚úì (RATIONALE-justified: neutral and universal across Spanish-speaking countries)

**STATUS**: ‚ö†Ô∏è CRITICAL INCONSISTENCY - Multiple different terms in use across apps!

**ANALYSIS**:
All three terms are valid in Spanish education:
- "Hoja de ejercicios" = Sheet of exercises (literal, descriptive)
- "Ficha" = Worksheet/activity sheet (common in Spain & LATAM, concise)
- "Ficha de trabajo" = Work sheet (explicit, used in schools)

**RECOMMENDATION**: **"Ficha"** (Addition's choice)
- Most concise and natural
- Widely used across Spain and Latin America
- Common in educational software
- More user-friendly than longer alternatives

**CRITICAL FINDINGS FROM CHART COUNT ANALYSIS**:
Cross-app grep revealed MASSIVE inconsistency:
- **"Ficha"** ‚Üí Addition, Chart Count (now), Draw-and-Color (now), Grid Match (now), Missing Pieces (now)
- **"Ficha de trabajo"** ‚Üí Big-Small, Pattern Train
- **"Ficha de ejercicios"** ‚Üí Math Puzzle, Prepositions (RATIONALE-justified), Code Addition, Sudoku
- **"Ficha de Actividades"** ‚Üí Shadow Match
- **"Hoja de trabajo"** ‚Üí Alphabet Train, Crossword (and Chart Count, Grid Match, Missing Pieces before fix)
- **"Hoja de ejercicios"** ‚Üí Cryptogram (and Draw-and-Color before fix)

**NEXT STEPS**:
1. **URGENT**: Platform-wide standardization needed
2. Recommended standard: "Ficha" (most concise, natural, widely used)
3. Need to update ~20+ apps to consistent terminology

- ‚úÖ Grid Match ACTUAL: Updated to SMART PATTERN ‚≠ê - "Respuestas" for tab (line 679, was "Soluciones"), "Hoja de respuestas" in full contexts (lines 677, 682, 684, 689, 691, 707)
- ‚úÖ Missing Pieces ACTUAL: Updated to SMART PATTERN ‚≠ê - "Respuestas" for tab (line 813), "Hoja de respuestas" in full contexts (lines 733-734, 738, 746-747)

**STATUS**: ‚ö†Ô∏è VARIATION FOUND - But Chart Count demonstrates EXCELLENT UX pattern

**ANALYSIS**:
- "Hoja de respuestas" = Answer sheet (literal, clear) - 2 apps use this
- "Solucionario" = Answer key/solution book (formal) - 1 app uses this

**RECOMMENDATION**: **SMART PATTERN DISCOVERED** ‚≠ê
Chart Count demonstrates excellent UX:
- **Tab labels**: Use short form "Respuestas" (concise for UI)
- **Full contexts**: Use complete form "Hoja de respuestas" (clear in buttons/messages)

This dual approach provides:
- Better UI economy in space-constrained tabs
- Full clarity in action contexts

**CROSS-APP GREP FINDINGS**:
- "Hoja de respuestas" ‚Üí Majority of apps (Big-Small, Code Addition, Crossword, Cryptogram, Find Objects, Grid Match, Math Puzzle, Missing Pieces, Pattern Train, Prepositions (full contexts), Sudoku, etc.)
- "Solucionario" ‚Üí Odd One Out, Word Guess
- "Respuestas" (short) ‚Üí Chart Count (tabs), Grid Match (tabs), Math Puzzle (tabs), More-Less

**SMART PATTERN ADOPTION**:
- ‚úÖ Chart Count: Introduced dual-form pattern (short tabs, full contexts)
- ‚úÖ Grid Match: Applied Chart Count pattern (line 679)
- ‚úÖ Math Puzzle: Applied Chart Count pattern (line 767)
- ‚úÖ Missing Pieces: Applied Chart Count pattern (line 813)

**NEXT STEPS**:
1. **Consider adopting Chart Count's smart pattern platform-wide**
2. Standardize to "Hoja de respuestas" for full contexts
3. Allow "Respuestas" for tab labels (UI economy)

## Spanish - Find Objects Unique Terminology

**Game-Specific Terms** (Unique to Find Objects / I Spy activities):

1. **"Elementos distractores"** (Distractors)
   - Objects that are NOT the search targets (background complexity)
   - Professional pedagogical term in Spanish
   - Clear distinction from "Objetos a encontrar"
   - Lines: 742, 748, 761, 774

2. **"Objetos a encontrar"** (Objects to Find)
   - The actual search targets
   - More natural than literal "Objetos ocultos" (hidden objects)
   - Clearer for Spanish-speaking children and teachers
   - Lines: 746, 749, 762, 775

3. **"BuscaObras"** (App Name)
   - Creative Spanish adaptation of "SpotWorks"
   - Combines "Buscar" (to search) + "Obras" (works)
   - Maintains creative educational tone
   - Natural Spanish word formation
   - Line: 671-672

**QUALITY ASSESSMENT**:
- ‚úÖ Native Spanish feel: Excellent
- ‚úÖ Professional trust: High - appropriate for kindergarten teachers
- ‚úÖ Educational appropriateness: Perfect - matches Spanish "busca y encuentra" activities
- ‚úÖ Regional compatibility: Neutral Spanish, works across all regions

**STATUS**: ‚úÖ All app-specific terminology approved - Professional and culturally appropriate

**IMPLEMENTATION NOTES**:
- Use "Genera" for button labels (e.g., "Genera scheda")
- Use "generato" in success messages (e.g., "Scheda generata con successo!")
- Use "Genera prima" in instructions (e.g., "Genera prima una scheda esercizi")
- Use "Generazione" for ongoing processes (e.g., "Generazione dati del rompicapo...")
- Consistent across all contexts

## Portuguese (Brazilian) - "Gerund Forms (Progressive Tense)"

**PLATFORM STANDARD**: **Use Gerund (-ndo) not "A + infinitive"**

**RATIONALE**:
- Brazilian Portuguese prefers gerund for progressive actions
- European Portuguese uses "A + infinitive" construction
- Example: "Carregando..." (BR) vs "A carregar..." (PT)
- More natural and modern in Brazilian usage
- SOURCE: Grid Match Brazilian conversion (2025-11-29)

**APPS ANALYZED** (13/33):
- ‚úÖ Grid Match ACTUAL: Updated to gerund forms
- Lines 1019, 1102-1108 (Carregando, Preparando, Pesquisando, Processando)

**STATUS**: ‚úÖ Platform standard established - Use gerund

**IMPLEMENTATION NOTES**:
- Loading: "Carregando..." (not "A carregar...")
- Preparing: "Preparando..." (not "A preparar...")
- Searching: "Pesquisando..." (not "A pesquisar...")
- Processing: "Processando..." (not "A processar...")

- More natural Brazilian construction

### Danish - "Opacity"

**PLATFORM STANDARD**: **"Gennemsigtighed"** (Transparency - native Danish)

**RATIONALE**:
- Native Danish word (more user-friendly than Latin "transparens")
- Used by 17+ apps including: Pattern Worksheet, Cryptogram, Code Addition, Find Objects, Matchup Maker, Crossword, Alphabet Train, Drawing Lines, Grid Match, Missing Pieces, Draw and Color, Coloring, Picture Sort, Writing, Addition, Math Puzzle
- Compound forms: "Baggrundsgennemsigtighed", "Rammegennemsigtighed"
- Follows German pattern: "Transparenz" (accessible over technical)
- More natural for Danish kindergarten teachers

**RETROACTIVE FIXES APPLIED** (2025-11-30, during Pattern Worksheet analysis):
- ‚úÖ Chart Count: Line 1533 "Baggrundstransparens" ‚Üí "Baggrundsgennemsigtighed"
- ‚úÖ Chart Count: Line 1537 "Rammetransparens" ‚Üí "Rammegennemsigtighed"
- ‚úÖ Find and Count: Line 1304 "Baggrundstransparens" ‚Üí "Baggrundsgennemsigtighed"
- ‚úÖ Find and Count: Line 1311 "Rammetransparens" ‚Üí "Rammegennemsigtighed"
- ‚úÖ More-Less: Line 2784 "Baggrundstransparens" ‚Üí "Baggrundsgennemsigtighed"
- ‚úÖ More-Less: Line 2788 "Rammetransparens" ‚Üí "Rammegennemsigtighed"

**STANDARD REVISION NOTE**: Previous entry incorrectly stated "Transparens" as standard. Corrected to "Gennemsigtighed" based on actual app survey (17+ apps use native Danish term).

### Norwegian - "Opacity"

**PLATFORM STANDARD**: ‚úÖ **"Synlighet"** (ADOPTED 2025-12-01)
**PREVIOUS STANDARD**: "Gjennomsiktighet" (5 apps, 2025-11-27 to 2025-12-01)
**ALTERNATIVE CONSIDERED**: "Dekkevne" (Wordsearch/Glossary recommendation)

**RATIONALE FOR STANDARD CHANGE**:
- **"Synlighet"** = visibility (most user-friendly, least technical)
- "Gjennomsiktighet" = transparency (inverse concept, more technical)
- "Dekkevne" = covering ability (most technical, less common)
- **Math Puzzle analysis provided compelling evidence** for superior user-friendliness
- **Aligns perfectly with platform philosophy**: "user-friendly over technical"
- **Best for target audience**: kindergarten teachers understand "visibility" immediately

## Finnish - Page Format Terminology

**PLATFORM STANDARDS**:
- "Letter Pysty" - Letter Portrait (American format with Finnish orientation term)
- "A4 Pysty" - A4 Portrait (European format, dominant in Finland)
- "Vaaka" - Landscape (horizontal)
- "Pysty" - Portrait (vertical)
- "Mukautettu" - Custom

**RATIONALE**:
- Preserves "Letter" for American format recognition
- Uses Finnish terms "Pysty" (vertical) and "Vaaka" (horizontal)
- "Mukautettu" is standard Finnish software term
- SOURCE: Wordsearch RATIONALE lines 36-42

**APPS ANALYZED** (1/33):
- ‚úÖ Wordsearch: Uses standard format terminology (lines 2046-2050)

**STATUS**: ‚úÖ Baseline established

---

## Finnish - Translation Philosophy

**GUIDING PRINCIPLES**:
1. **Natural over literal** - App should feel originally Finnish
2. **Finnish educational context** - Use established pedagogical terminology
3. **Finnish UI conventions** - Respect Finnish software standards
4. **Clarity and accessibility** - Simple, unambiguous phrasing
5. **Terminological consistency** - Unified vocabulary throughout
6. **Modern Finnish** - Contemporary language use

**FORMALITY LEVEL**: "Sinuttelu" (informal "you")
- Modern standard for user interfaces
- More accessible and friendly
- Used consistently across all Finnish apps

**COMPOUND WORDS**: Proper Finnish formation
- Examples: "Sanaristikko", "Kuvakirjasto", "Tekstity√∂kalut"
- Hyphens used when needed for clarity: "Teht√§v√§arkki-generaattori"

**CASE GRAMMAR**: Correct use of Finnish's 15 cases
- Genitive: "Teht√§v√§arkin sis√§lt√∂kieli", "Kuvakirjaston kieli", "√Ñ√§riviivan v√§ri"
- Allative: "Kuval√§hde ristikolle"
- Illative: "Kohdista sivulle"
- Partitive: "Ladataan kuvia"

**VERB FORMS**:
- Passive for ongoing actions: "Ladataan..." (Loading...)
- Imperative for buttons: "Luo" (Create), "Lataa" (Download)
- No unnecessary nominalization

## Finnish - "Puzzle" (Word Scramble Context)

**CONTEXT-SPECIFIC STANDARD**: **"Pulma"** (for word scramble)

**RATIONALE**:
- "Pulma" is generic puzzle term, appropriate for word scrambles
- Different from "Ristikko" (grid-based puzzles like word search/crossword)
- Word scrambles are NOT grid-based, so "Pulma" is more appropriate
- SOURCE: Word Scramble RATIONALE line 83

**APPS ANALYZED**:
- ‚úÖ Word Scramble RATIONALE: Recommends "Pulma" for word scramble puzzles
- ‚úÖ Word Scramble ACTUAL: Uses "Pulma" (FIXED - was "Teht√§v√§")
- ‚úÖ Wordsearch: Uses "Ristikko" (grid puzzles) - CORRECT for that context

**STATUS**: ‚úÖ Context-appropriate terminology established

**NOTES**: 
- "Ristikko" for grid-based puzzles (word search, crossword)
- "Pulma" for non-grid puzzles (word scramble, anagram, etc.)
